	// http://www.javascripter.net/faq/rgbtohex.htm
	function rgbToHex(R,G,B) {return toHex(R)+toHex(G)+toHex(B)}
	function toHex(n) {
  n = parseInt(n,10);
  if (isNaN(n)) return "00";
  n = Math.max(0,Math.min(n,255));
  return "0123456789ABCDEF".charAt((n-n%16)/16)  + "0123456789ABCDEF".charAt(n%16);
	}

  var x = event.pageX - this.offsetLeft;

  var R = img_data[0];
  var G = img_data[1];
  var B = img_data[2];  
    var rgb = R + ',' + G + ',' + B;
  // convert RGB to HEX
  var hex = rgbToHex(R,G,B);
  // making the color the value of the input
  $('#rgb input').val(rgb);
  $('#hex input').val('#' + hex);

  function handleFiles(e) {
    var canvas = document.getElementById('canvas_picker');
    var ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  
    function createImage(zoomLevel, posX, posY) {
      var width = canvas.width + (zoomLevel * (canvas.width / canvas.height));
      var height = canvas.height + zoomLevel;
      var x = 0 - (posX / canvas.width) * (width - canvas.width);
      var y = 0 - (posY / canvas.height) * (height - canvas.height);
  
      var img = new Image();
      img.src = URL.createObjectURL(e.target.files[0]);
  
      img.onload = function() {
        $('#canvas_replace').hide();
        $('#canvas_picker').show();
        $('#input_box').show();
        ctx.drawImage(img, x, y, width, height);
      };
    }
  
    createImage(0, 0, 0);
  
    var x = 0, y = 0, zoomLevel = 0;
    
    canvas.onmousemove = function(e) {
      x = e.pageX - canvas.offsetLeft;
      y = e.pageY - canvas.offsetTop;
      createImage(zoomLevel, x, y);
    };
  
    canvas.onwheel = function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      var delta = e.wheelDelta ? e.wheelDelta : -e.deltaY;
      zoomLevel += delta > 0 ? 10 : -10;
      zoomLevel = Math.max(0, zoomLevel);
      createImage(zoomLevel, x, y);
    };
  }
